  <script type="text/javascript">
   var absoluteURL = "https://www.momastore.org/webapp/wcs/stores/servlet/";
var imageDirectoryPath = "/wcsstore/MOMASTORE1/";

//Summary: Returns the absolute URL to use for prefixing any Ajax URL call.
//Description: Dojo does not handle the case where the parameters in the URL are delimeted by the "/" forward slash. Therefore, in order to
//             workaround the issue, all AJAX requests must be done using absolute URLs rather than relative.
//Returns: The absolute URL to use for prefixing any Ajax URL call.
function getAbsoluteURL()
{
	if (absoluteURL != "") {
		absoluteURL = absoluteURL.replace("://momastore.org","://www.momastore.org");
		var currentURL = document.URL;
		var currentProtocol = "";
	
		if (currentURL.indexOf("://") != -1) {
			currentProtocol = currentURL.substring(0, currentURL.indexOf("://"));
		}
		
		var savedProtocol = "";
		if (absoluteURL.indexOf("://") != -1) {
			savedProtocol = absoluteURL.substring(0, absoluteURL.indexOf("://"));
		}
		
		if (currentProtocol != savedProtocol) {
			absoluteURL = currentProtocol + absoluteURL.substring(absoluteURL.indexOf("://"));
		}
	}
	
	return absoluteURL;
}
//Summary: Returns the path pointing to the shared image directory.
//Description: In order to get the image directory path in any javascript file, this function can be used.
//Returns: The path to reference images.
function getImageDirectoryPath()
{
	return imageDirectoryPath;
}
  </script>

	       "url":"/webapp/wcs/stores/servlet/MoMAENewsSubscription?storeId=10001",

	       "transition":"fadeIn",
	       "width":400,
	       "height":400
	     });
	}else{
	}
}

	var isOverlayEnabled = true    ;
	if(isOverlayEnabled == true &amp;&amp; document.location.href.indexOf("Sweepstakes")&lt;0){
		enewsOnLoad();
	}
});

function continueShoppingFn(){
	var lightboxScreen = dojo.byId("overlay-screen");
	var continueShopping = dojo.byId("continueShopping");
    dojo.style(lightboxScreen,'display','none');
    dojo.destroy(dojo.byId("overlay"));
}

    <script type="text/javascript">
     function addInputSubmitEvent(form, input) {
    input.onkeydown = function(e) {
        e = e || window.event;
        if (e.keyCode == 13 &amp;&amp; form.name=='LOGINFORM') {
            loginFromHeader(document.LOGINFORM);
            return false;
        }
    };
}

	dojo.addOnLoad(function() {
    	CommonControllersDeclarationJS.setControllerURL('MOMAHeaderDisplayController','MoMAHeaderDisplayView?langId=-1&amp;storeId=10001&amp;catalogId=10451');
    	var forms = document.getElementsByTagName('form');
		for (var i=0;i &lt; forms.length;i++) {
			if(forms[i].name =='LOGINFORM'){
	    	    var inputs = forms[i].getElementsByTagName('input');
			    for (var j=0;j &lt; inputs.length;j++)
				    addInputSubmitEvent(forms[i], inputs[j]);
			}    
    	}
    });
    </script>

   <meta content="In 1992 the MoMA Design Store introduced the Sky Umbrella by legendary graphic designer Tibor Kalman and Emanuela Frattini Magnusson. The umbrella's exterior gives away nothing more than a plain, black canopy and a simple wooden handle. Once opened, the interior reveals a cheerful blue sky dotted with fluffy, white clouds. The umbrella's surprising blue-sky interior echoes the playful career of Kalman, whose work is featured in the Museums collection. Kalman once again used the visual motif of the Sky Umbrella in a 1995 issue of &lt;i&gt;Colors&lt;/i&gt;, an award-winning global magazine where Kalman served as the founding editor-in-chief.     						    These thumbs contain html5 attributes data-* which are used to store
    						    the url of the medium image (520x520) and the larger image which appears
    						    on zoom (1500x1500)
    						    
    						    The zoomer will not work with out these attributes.
    						    
    						    Furthermore, it may be the case that there are products which do not have
    						    a larger image in which case the zoomer will not be triggered. Those images
    						    will not have the required data- attribute.
    						    
    						    From a javascript perspective, to distinguish between images that can be zoomed 
    						    and those that cannot, you *must* add a class of "zoomable" to those images that
    						    can be zoomed. 
    						    
    						    This is illustrated in the code sample below 						    
    						    -->

       <div class="clearfix" id="product-description">
        <h3 class="clearfix">
         Product Description
        </h3>
        <h2 class="clearfix">
         Sky Umbrella
        </h2>
        <p>
         <img alt="" onerror="this.src='/wcsstore/MOMASTORE1/images/products/NoImage_white.jpg'" src="/wcsstore/MOMASTORE1/images/products/about/31587_DescriptionImage.jpg"/>
         In 1992 the MoMA Design Store introduced the Sky Umbrella by legendary graphic designer Tibor Kalman and Emanuela Frattini Magnusson. The umbrella's exterior gives away nothing more than a plain, black canopy and a simple wooden handle. Once opened, the interior reveals a cheerful blue sky dotted with fluffy, white clouds. The umbrella's surprising blue-sky interior echoes the playful career of Kalman, whose work is featured in the Museums collection. Kalman once again used the visual motif of the Sky Umbrella in a 1995 issue of
         <i>
          Colors
         </i>
         , an award-winning global magazine where Kalman served as the founding editor-in-chief. Made of sturdy nylon covering the photo-process-printed sky on polyester with a durable wooden shaft and handle with a manual open/close mechanism.
         <br/>
         <br/>
         <b>
          Shop the Collapsible Sky Umbrella
          <a href="http://www.momastore.org/museum/moma/ProductDisplay?storeId=10001&amp;catalogId=10451&amp;langId=-1&amp;categoryId=11507&amp;parent_category_rn=26715&amp;productId=46251&amp;keyWord=Sky%20Umbrella,%20Collapsible&amp;purpose=crawl" target="new">
           here
          </a>
          .
         </b>
        </p>
        <!-- Handling hidden category -->
        <a class="arrow-right" href="CategoryDisplay_10451_10001_11470_11470_-1_Y_Best Sellers">
         <span class="uppercase">
          View more Best Sellers
         </span>
        </a>
        <!-- Handling hidden category -->
       </div>
       <!--  Multi valued Lego changes -->
       <div class="clearfix" id="about-the-designer">
        <h3>
         About the Designer
        </h3>
        <h2>
         Tibor Kalman
        </h2>
        <p>
         <img alt="" height="283" src="/wcsstore/MOMASTORE1/images/legos/images/kalman.jpg" width="220"/>
         Tibor Kalman (1949-1999) founded the legendary, multidisciplinary design firm M&amp;Co in 1979. In collaboration with his wife Maira, the conceptually progressive firm initially created graphics, magazines and film titles, and books. Following the release of a record album cover for the rock band Talking Heads, M&amp;Co gained major attention for "pushing the envelope" on conventions of design and typography, and went on to become a major influence on emerging designers.
        </p>
        <a class="arrow-right" href="/museum/moma/CategoryDisplay_10451_10001_11476_11571_-1_Y_Tibor%20Kalman">
         <span class="uppercase">
          View more by this designer
         </span>
        </a>
       </div>

I liked it so much I bought a second as a gift for a family member.  Very disappointing when the box was opened to reveal an umbrella broken in half.  Adding insult to injury is that it must have been boxed that way since the umbrella was wrapped in bubble wrap and the box was in fine condition.

              <div class="pr-review-text">
               <p class="pr-comments-header">
                Comments about
                <em>
                 <span class="pr-product-name">
                  Sky Umbrella
                 </span>
                </em>
                :
               </p>
               <p class="pr-comments">
                This is a beautiful umbrella. Lovely wooden handle, double lined, so more resident to being damaged by the wind. However it does not open automatically, which in this day and age is not only unusual, but also unnecessary. To prove that point there are other, very similar umbrellas on the market that do open automatically, so there really is no need to purchase this one. Alas, I did not read the description sufficiently to work that out before ordering. I would return it, but being based in the UK the cost of the return postage makes that pointless in terms of recouping the price of the umbrella. My mistake, but it honestly didn't occur to me that anyone even made manual opening full sized umbrellas anymore.
               </p>
              </div>

	function prLoginCreate(theForm, returnURL){
	    var url = dojo.byId("MoMALoginForPRURL").value;
		url += "&amp;catentryId="+ theForm.coloroptions.value;
	    url += "&amp;returnURL=" + returnURL;
		if(theForm.name == "productDetailDisplay"){	  
	        MOMA.lightbox({
	        	"url": url,
	        	"onSuccess": MOMA.lightboxEvents.switchToLogin,
	        	"transition":"fadeIn"
	        });
        }else{
	        MOMA.lightbox({
	        	"url": url,
	        	"onSuccess": MOMA.lightboxEvents.switchToLogin,
	        	"transition":"resize"
	        });
        }
	}
